         <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
          <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.mmafighting.com/2021/3/21/22342721/dana-white-says-kevin-holland-had-mental-breakdown-in-main-event-derek-brunson-disagrees">
           Dana White says Kevin Holland had ‘mental breakdown’ in main event; Derek Brunson disagrees
          </a>
         </h2>
         <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
          UFC president Dana White was not impressed by what he saw out of Kevin Holland on Saturday night as the always outspoken middleweight never stopped talking but ultimately lost a lopsided decision to Derek Brunson.
         </p>

            </time>

        <div class="c-entry-box--compact__body">
         <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
          <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.mmafighting.com/2021/3/21/22342711/khabib-nurmagomedov-never-contemplated-return-from-retirement-says-he-has-nothing-to-prove">
           Khabib Nurmagomedov never contemplated return from retirement, says he has nothing to prove
          </a>
         </h2>
         <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
          Khabib Nurmagomedov announced his retirement this past October and it turns out he never actually contemplated a comeback because in his mind, he has absolutely nothing left to prove.
         </p>
         <div class="c-byline" data-cdata='{"timestamp":1616328000}' data-cid="site/byline-1616397905_3343_1034333">
          <span class="c-byline-wrapper">

         <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
          <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.mmafighting.com/2021/3/21/22342712/kevin-holland-eyes-welterweight-fight-with-belal-muhammad-why-not-do-it-now">
           Kevin Holland eyes welterweight fight with Belal Muhammad: ‘Why not do it now?’
          </a>
         </h2>
         <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
          A 25-minute fight with Derek Brunson served as a reckoning for Kevin Holland at UFC Vegas 22.
         </p>
         <div class="c-byline" data-cdata='{"timestamp":1616353200}' data-cid="site/byline-1616397905_543_1034339">

         <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
          <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.mmafighting.com/2021/3/21/22342588/alexander-volkanovski-gutted-after-covid-19-positive-test-caused-ufc-260-scratch">
           Alexander Volkanovski ‘gutted’ after COVID-19 positive test caused UFC 260 scratch
          </a>
         </h2>
         <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
          The featherweight champ revealed the reason for his removal from a UFC 260 title fight against Brian Ortega.
         </p>
         <div class="c-byline" data-cdata='{"timestamp":1616342400}' data-cid="site/byline-1616397905_5582_1034345">
          <span class="c-byline-wrapper">

             </span>

            </time>
           </span>

         <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
          <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.mmafighting.com/2021/3/21/22336610/georges-st-pierre-advises-conor-mcgregor-to-get-out-his-comfort-zone-or-you-will-go-down">

         </p>

        <div class="c-entry-box--compact__body">
         <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
          <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.mmafighting.com/2021/3/21/22334620/frank-mir-has-nothing-but-love-for-jake-pauls-venture-into-boxing">
           Frank Mir has ‘nothing but love’ for Jake Paul’s venture into boxing
          </a>
         </h2>
         <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
          Frank Mir sees a lot of positives in YouTube star Jake Paul becoming a big name in combat sports.
         </p>
         <div class="c-byline" data-cdata='{"timestamp":1616349600}' data-cid="site/byline-1616397905_1306_1034357">
          <span class="c-byline-wrapper">

            </time>

            <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">

              UFC Vegas 22 results: Montserrat Ruiz outgrapples Cheyanne Buys to win in octagon debut
             </a>
            </h2>
            <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">

               <span data-chorus-optimize-field="hed">
                RIZIN 27 results, videos: Ayaka Hamasaki retains belt in night of quick finishes
               </span>
               <span class="c-rock-list__entry-blurb">
                RIZIN 27 featured knockouts that have entered the company’s record books.

             </a>
            </h2>
            <p class="p-dek c-entry-box--compact__dek" data-chorus-optimize-field="dek">
             Seven years ago, doctors told former UFC lightweight Spencer Fisher he could no longer fight. That wasn’t the end of his time with his promoter. But when the company was sold, he was among those to be cut loose. Now, he’s just trying to get by.
            </p>
            <div class="c-byline" data-cdata='{"timestamp":1610460000}' data-cid="site/byline-1616396688_6482_52073">
             <span class="c-byline-wrapper">

              <span class="c-byline__item">

                </span>
               </a>
              </span>
              <span class="c-byline__item">
               <time class="c-byline__item" data-relative-timestamp="true" data-ui="timestamp" datetime="2021-01-12T14:00:00">
                January 12
               </time>

           <div class="c-entry-box--compact__body">
            <h2 class="c-entry-box--compact__title">
             <a data-analytics-link="article" data-chorus-optimize-field="hed" href="https://www.mmafighting.com/2021/3/20/22337807/trevin-giles-explains-to-critics-dana-white-why-he-really-fainted-at-ufc-vegas-5">

    // will load outbrain if openmic doesn't get loaded in 2s
    //
    var adBlockerTimeoutId = setTimeout(loadOutbrain, 5000);
    document.body.addEventListener('first_ad_rendered', function(){
      clearTimeout(adBlockerTimeoutId);
      var outbrainTimeoutId = setTimeout(loadOutbrain, 2000);
      document.body.addEventListener('playlistRendered', function(){
        clearTimeout(outbrainTimeoutId);
      });
    });
  }
})();
    </script>
